1935.03.24

Yellow River Blocking Project: Kong and Li in Charge of Separate Sections; Hebei Provincial Government Convened a Blocking Conference; 3,800 Yuan Allocated for Emergency Rescue

(Tianjin) The Yellow River's water level has risen sharply, making the blocking project urgent. A new engineering office has been formed, with Kong Xianrong responsible for handling the Guantai Gou and Jinmen Ka blocking projects. Li Yizhi is specifically responsible for repairing the Taihang and Jin dikes and rescuing the areas south of Hebei. Hu Yuanhui, the Director of the Hebei Construction Department, is at the construction site and no longer has any responsibility. He will return to Tianjin within the next week. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the 23rd, the Hebei Provincial Government convened a conference of various departments to discuss blocking the Yellow River. All department heads attended, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Send a telegram to the magistrate of Changyuan County, urging him to supervise the workers to spare no effort in the blocking efforts, and to formulate methods for rescuing the Taihang and Jin dikes. (2) Send a telegram to the bureau chief, ordering him to meet with the county to survey and set up defenses. (3) Allocate 3,800 yuan from the Yellow River disaster relief funds and remit it to Changyuan for emergency rescue use. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the 23rd, the Provincial Government received a telegram from Zhang Qinglu, the magistrate of Changyuan County, stating that the wind had subsided slightly on the 22nd, and the water level had not risen or fallen. Although the danger to the measured dike had been averted, rescue efforts were still needed as the situation demanded. He requested an allocation of 5,300 yuan for purchasing materials. The Hebei Construction Department purchased 5,000 burlap sacks, which were transported to the Yellow River work site on the 23rd for use. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The water level at the Guantai breach of the Yellow River continues to rise, and the situation regarding the blocking project is becoming increasingly critical. Moreover, strong spring winds have been frequent in recent days, causing turbulent waves. The Taihang Dike and the defenses of Changyuan City are under increasing pressure. Furthermore, the Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram on the 23rd from Ye Zhenmin, the surveyor dispatched to Guantai, reporting that refugees are flocking to the disaster area, with people in the surrounding villages having no clothes or food and urgently needing relief. Currently, the number of refugees in Changyuan County has reached 140,000. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) Kong Xianrong went to Zhengzhou on the morning of the 23rd to request that the Pinghan Railway allocate trains from Heshan Bridge and the Longhai Railway from Xuzhou to transport stone materials, both starting on the 24th. (23rd Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) In the past two years, the Yellow River has caused more than 14,000 deaths and losses of more than 30 million yuan in Hua County. (23rd Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) Chang Zhichen returned to Bian on the evening of the 22nd. According to his account: (1) He met with Wang Jingwei and Xu Chongzhi in Beijing, who promised to find ways to provide relief funds for Henan. (2) He planned to establish a Henan Mining Industry Bank in Shanghai, but due to the economic depression, it is unlikely to succeed. (3) He planned to build a cement plant at Tiemen, which will only be decided after a survey by a Swiss company. (23rd Dispatch)

(Jinan) Zhao Mingyuan, the Director of the Immigration Reclamation Office, came to Qi today to meet with Zhang Honglie, the Director of the Construction Department, to urge the relocation of disaster victims to repair the Yellow River's tail reach civil embankments and block the Jingzikou breach to protect the reclamation area. Zhao said that there are currently 4,000 disaster victims from western Shandong who have voluntarily gone to northern Shandong for reclamation. (23rd Dispatch)

Zhang Jingjiang and Others Arrived in Hankou; Going to Sichuan at Jiang's Invitation; Chen Bulei Flew to Sichuan Yesterday

(Hankou) Zhang Jingjiang, Li Shizeng, and Wu Jingheng, three members of the Central Supervisory Committee, were invited by Jiang via telegram to go to Sichuan for discussions and sightseeing. They arrived in Hankou at 7:30 AM on the 23rd aboard the Yongnian transport ship and took the same ship to Yichang at 5 PM in the afternoon, transferring to another ship to Sichuan. (23rd Dispatch)

(Hankou) After the three members of the Central Supervisory Committee, Wu, Li, and Zhang, arrived in Hankou, Zhang Xueliang and Zhang Qun boarded the ship to pay their respects. Wu and the others then went ashore to inspect the municipal administration of Hankou. They departed westward at 5 PM that evening. Wu said that this trip to Chongqing was for sightseeing. After meeting with Jiang, they would go to Chengdu, and he would travel to Mount Emei alone. Li and Zhang would return to Shanghai from Chengdu. (23rd Dispatch)

(Hankou) Chen Bulei flew to Sichuan on the morning of the 23rd aboard the Kangdao plane, accompanied by Chen Qiuyang, Xie Linxue, and Mrs. Yan Daogang. He arrived in Chongqing in the afternoon and resided in Taoyuan to work. (23rd Dispatch)

Liu Luyin Arrived in Guangzhou

(Hong Kong) Liu Luyin arrived in Guangdong Province, paid respects to Chen Jitang, and reported to committee members such as Xiao Focheng and Zou Lu on the progress of negotiations in Beijing. He also carried handwritten letters from central dignitaries to be delivered to Chen Jitang and others. (23rd Dispatch)

Our Protest Against the Sino-Soviet Railway; The Russian Side Has Not Responded

(Nanjing) The illegal sale of the Sino-Soviet Railway was signed in Japan on the morning of the 23rd. The Russian side has not provided a written or oral response to our letter of protest. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that our legal procedures have been completed and that there is no need to reiterate the protest. Therefore, it takes a nonchalant view of the illegal signing. (23rd Dispatch)

Sichuan New Life Movement Established; Chairman Chiang Personally Gave Instructions; Cleanliness Parade Held in the Afternoon

(Chongqing) The Sichuan Provincial New Life Movement Promotion Association held its inaugural meeting at 10:00 AM on the 23rd. Over 1,600 people attended, including Chief Director Liu Xiang, Executive Directors Xie Zuomin and Li Genggu, and Directors Kang Ze, Yang Quanyu, and Gan Jiyong. Chairman Chiang personally gave instructions, his words being earnest and sincere, lasting for over an hour. In the afternoon, a cleanliness parade was held by people from all walks of life. Before the departure, Xie Zuomin personally provided guidance and explained the meaning of the New Life Movement in detail. During the meeting, airplanes scattered tens of thousands of leaflets, and shops and organizations hung flags to celebrate. The atmosphere throughout Chongqing was completely renewed. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Agricultural Loan Group; Invited Pingyin Bankers to Talk

(Beiping) The China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Group held a discussion meeting with representatives from various banks at the Bank Association at 10:00 AM on the morning of the 23rd. Zhou Zuomin, Leng Jiaji, and others attended to discuss all relevant matters. They planned to establish offices in Zhengzhou and Xi'an to oversee cooperative loan operations. The Ping office nominated the China South Bank to be responsible for preparations. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Economic Commission Dispatched Survey Teams; To Assist in Surveying Fujian Province Highways

(Nanjing) Following Chairman Chiang's previous telegram, the Highway Bureau of the Economic Commission dispatched two survey teams to assist in surveying the highways of Fujian, Shaxian, Yongding, Liancheng, Shanghang. The two teams have now been formed and are leaving for Fujian immediately. In addition, the Gansu-Xinjiang Highway Survey Team organized by the commission is about to be completed and will depart at the end of the month. (23rd Dispatch)

Tax Dispute Between Mongolia and Sui Province Being Mediated; Rumors of Conflict Between Mongolian and Sui Province Armies Unconfirmed; Bao Yueqing Visited He Yingqin Yesterday to Report the Truth

(Beiping) The tax dispute between Mongolia and Sui Province has intensified. Since Prince De sent a telegram to Xiao Renyuan expressing a complete rejection of the previously agreed-upon resolution at Bailingmiao, there have been widespread rumors here last night of certain actions being taken by both sides. However, it has been learned that this is not the case, although there have been troop movements by both sides. The Sui Province army has approximately two regiments stationed in the Heishata area, while the Mongolian army has approximately 500 men. Prince De has recently returned to Bailingmiao from Heishata, so the situation is still relatively calm. This confirms that the rumors are not true. In order to prevent the situation from escalating, He Yingqin summoned Bao Yueqing, Prince De's representative in Beiping, this morning and informed him that a resolution principle had been established for the dispute. He ordered Bao to immediately telegram Prince De, hoping that Prince De would resolve the issue peacefully, upholding his past loyalty to the Central Government. After taking his leave, Bao telegraphed Prince De and expected a reply to arrive in Beiping tomorrow. According to Bao, the issue should be resolved within a few days. Xiao Zhenying has also been working with all relevant parties on this matter today, with good progress. Xiao may travel to Bailingmiao after gaining some insight. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Bao Yueqing said, "I received a telegram from Prince De this morning, reporting that the Sui Province army has suddenly increased its forces in Asak to around two regiments. Asak is about 500 li northwest of Bailingmiao. I reported to He and requested that he take immediate measures to prevent misunderstandings. I reported everything to He this morning, and He stated that he would definitely take appropriate measures. I have already telegraphed Prince De to report He's intentions." (23rd Dispatch)

Guihua: Fu Zuoyi sent Li Juyi, Director of the Finance Department, to Beiping on the 23rd to meet with He Yingqin to discuss resolving the tax dispute between Sui and Mongolia. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Security Team in the Miyun Area; Pursuing and Suppressing Rebel Police with Machine Guns; Yin Rugeng Obtained Japanese Approval; Japanese Army at Gubeikou Jointly Blocking

(Beiping) Miyun telephone: About two hundred members of Feng Shoupeng's rebel force broke through Malanyu and crossed the Great Wall, then returned to Miyun via Qiangzilu. Our security team immediately surrounded them from the east, south, and west. Because our security team could not advance to the north, the rebels broke through from the north and arrived at a place about one li outside Shixia Town on the morning of the 22nd, cutting the telephone lines and disrupting communication between Beiping and Gubeikou. The security teams of Miyun, Zunhua, and Beiping-Gubeikou counties continued their suppression, engaging in fierce battles, killing dozens of rebels and one security police officer. By evening, the rebels were unable to hold out and retreated twenty li to the west, now in the Donggezhuang area, with a tendency to flee outside the pass. The Japanese army at Gubeikou, upon receiving the news, also dispatched troops to block the passes at Baimaguan and other places. The rebel forces should be resolved within a day or two. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zunhua telephone: After the Zunhua security team was transferred to Miyun to assist in suppressing the rebels, the police force became somewhat thin. On the evening of the 22nd, a group of rebels suddenly rushed into the second district of Zunhua County from the Rehe area, confiscating some of the militia's firearms. The militia police are now jointly suppressing the rebels. The rebels are carrying machine guns, and Yin Rugeng, after being informed, went to the Japanese Embassy this morning to visit Japanese military attache Takahashi to discuss transporting a machine gun unit to the war zone to enable the security team to quickly clear the rebel scourge. It is hoped that there will be no problems after the rebels are quelled before they are removed. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Feng Shoupeng's unit only started to be reorganized on the 22nd. Zhao Lei ordered the officers and soldiers of the unit not to leave the team without permission before the reorganization was completed. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) After the rebel soldiers of Feng Shoupeng's unit fled to Miyun, they caused great disturbances in the local area. The Ji-Miyun District Office has recently agreed with the Japanese side to allow the security team to temporarily carry six machine guns to suppress the rebels. It is expected that they can be completely annihilated within a few days. The telephone lines between Miyun and Gubeikou, which were cut off by the rebels, have now been repaired by dispatched workers. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Miyun telephone: When the rebel soldiers of Feng Shoupeng's unit were west of Shixia at Donggezhuang last night, they were tracked and pursued by the security team to the Taiziling area, where one rebel was captured, along with a large gun, a bicycle, and one rebel was killed. One person was captured alive, several rebels were wounded, and several mules and horses were seized. Two hostages were rescued. The Japanese army at Gubeikou dispatched troops to defend at Baimaguan. The Japanese side contacted Zhang Wen, the magistrate of Miyun County, by telephone to agree on a joint suppression. Feng's rebels are still hiding in the Xiaoshijian Mountain. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) The unresolved issues in the Hebei war zone, after being discussed and decided by personnel from both China and Japan in Tianjin, are being handled in three steps. The first step, the issue of the Yutian security team being transferred, has been completed. The Feng Shoupeng unit transferred to Tangshan is undergoing training. The Sun Jizhou unit transferred to the Tongxian-Sanhe border area is being reorganized and trained under the command of General Team Leader Li Yuncheng, as ordered by the Ji-Miyun District Office. The second step, the issue of the new security team entering the area, is still under slight revision because we have 9,000 trained men, but only 5,000 are being deployed. The deployment is expected to be negotiated and finalized after Yu Xuezhong returns to Tianjin. The third step, the issue of receiving Malanyu Dongling, has been referred to the Japanese Kwantung Army by Japanese military attache Takahashi. The Japanese side has proposed conditions, such as resolving issues related to the protection of Dongling before it can be returned. This issue is being negotiated with the Japanese side by Gu Rugeng and others, and it will take some time. There are approximately 20,000 impoverished descendants of the Qing dynasty in Dongling. They established a Forestry Reclamation Bureau and cleared the forests in the area from Dongling to Xinglong, which took seven or eight years, showing the extent of the loss. The Ji-Miyun District Office plans to carry out afforestation and farming after receiving Dongling to provide a livelihood for tens of thousands of Banner people. However, how to raise this funding is still a matter of concern. (23rd Dispatch)

Dagdong Company in Yuguan to Resell Exit Permits

(Beiping) The Japanese Dagdong Company in Yuguan issued a notice on the 20th of this month, stating that the company had previously been ordered to stop selling "entry permits" in accordance with the regulations for the control of foreigners entering the country. Now, they have been ordered to resume the sale of "entry permits" from April 1st, which will be sold by both the company and the Japanese Military Police in Yuguan for 3 jiao each. However, people entering the country must first fill out their resumes at the company or the military police station. It is heard that the Japanese were preventing Chinese from leaving the customs, and after negotiations between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the relevant authorities in North China, the Japanese side agreed to postpone it for one year. Therefore, the Dagdong Company in Yuguan was ordered to implement it. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) On the 23rd, the Beiping-Shenyang Railway Bureau submitted a report detailing the investigation of the false police in Shanhaiguan preventing Chinese from leaving the customs, to the Military Branch and the Ministry of Railways, requesting instructions for compliance. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Passengers who were prevented from leaving the customs in Yuguan and returned their tickets on the section outside the customs are currently being handled by the Yuguan ticket office of the Tian-Beiping Railway Bureau. The accounts will be settled with the Oriental Travel Agency later. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) There have been few travelers going to the Northeast on the Beiping-Shenyang train in recent days. The train that left this morning had only 25 passengers. However, when the Beiping-Shenyang train arrived in Beiping last night, there was a large influx of people entering the country, about 250 people. (23rd Dispatch)

Reorganization Plan for Oriental Travel Agency; Will Be Implemented Next Month

(Tianjin) The reorganization plan for the Oriental Travel Agency has been largely finalized. The International Tourism Bureau will still be responsible for it in the coming days. Deputy Manager Hirayama will remain in place. After our side, the China Travel Agency, withdraws, Zhang Shuiqi and personnel familiar with the transportation industry will form a Chinese capital group for the Beiping-Shenyang special express train. The reorganization is expected to be realized around the 15th of next month. The Japanese side objects to changing the name and having private individuals take over the Oriental Travel Agency. Therefore, our country is forming a capital group to be responsible for the travel agency. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The capital of the Oriental Travel Agency is currently set at 2 million yuan to purchase two trains and build a railway hotel in Shanhaiguan. It was agreed to raise one-quarter of the capital first. Subsequently, after starting the business, only one-eighth of the capital was raised, with China and Japan each responsible for 125,000 yuan, which has been used up in losses in the past six months. After the reorganization, the remaining capital will continue to be paid up and stored in the company for future use. As for purchasing trains, we have rejected the Japanese proposal due to issues of sovereignty and complex relationships. Zhang Shuiqi may go to Beiping at the end of the month to meet with Yin Tong to discuss everything in advance. The operating expenses of the Oriental Travel Agency in the past were too high, with ordinary employee salaries exceeding 200 yuan. After the reorganization, this may be reduced. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) A reorganization meeting for the Oriental Travel Agency will be held in Beiping on the 5th of next month, with Yin Tong, Takahashi, Hirayama, and Zhang Shuiqi as the central figures for negotiations between China and Japan. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Oriental Travel Agency and the Beiping-Shenyang Railway Bureau have agreed that passengers who were prevented from leaving the customs in Shanhaiguan can get a full refund for their tickets for the Yuguan-Shenyang section at the ticket office of Shanhaiguan Station. The handling fee charged by the railway bureau will be waived. Since the 21st, the situation of the pseudo-border police preventing passengers from leaving the customs has eased slightly. However, there are still thousands of passengers staying in the Yutai Hotel in Yuguan, waiting for letters of certification from relatives and friends outside the customs as proof to leave. Large and small hotels and inns are overcrowded. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The pseudo-Dagdong Company in Shanhaiguan posted a notice on the 22nd, stating that it had previously been ordered to stop issuing entry permits and that it would resume the old method of selling them from April 1st, charging 5 jiao per permit. However, when purchasing, one must attach proof and the permission of the Japanese Military Police. The Beiping-Shenyang Railway Bureau denies that it is providing free transportation back to Beiping and Tianjin for passengers prevented from leaving the customs in Yuguan. (23rd Dispatch)

Liu Guitang's Bandit Gang Raiding Sanhe County

(Tianjin) A part of Liu Guitang's bandit gang arrived in Sanhe County on the 22nd, looting villages. The Yingjiapu militia has gone to suppress them. Kuwata, a sergeant from the Tangshan Japanese army, has gone to the Lincangzhen in Yutian to investigate the reorganization of the militia. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Wang Qingfang part of Liu Guitang's bandit gang, after being pursued and suppressed by Wang Zhanyuan's part of Zunhua security team, has arrived at the Great Wall line of Huanghuashan Bangchuishan. The Japanese army has counterattacked, with more than ten casualties. The pursuit is still in progress. (23rd Dispatch)

Zhou Yuying's Security Team Surrounding Yajiangqiao Town; Stalemated with the Militia

(Tianjin) Over three hundred members of Zhou Yuying's security team in Yutian surrounded the Sun Chengzong's part of the militia in Yajiangqiao Town on the 21st, planning to disarm and disperse the force. The militia is holding the town and guarding it, and the two sides are stalemated. The situation is dangerous, and local gentry are trying their best to mediate. The security third general team has disarmed six or seven tenths of Yutian's militias. Only a small portion is unwilling to comply. On the 22nd, Zhao Cong'an, the county magistrate, convened a meeting of gentry in the county to discuss methods for forming a legal militia, with a quota of approximately 2,000 men in one general team and four major parts. (23rd Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhou Yuying, the commander of the 3rd Security General Detachment of the war zone, passed through Tianjin on the 23rd to go to Beiping to meet with He Yingqin to report on the progress of the Yutian Tuandfang. According to him, Yutian has become peaceful, and merchants who fled have gradually returned, and many shops have reopened. All the county's militias have peacefully accepted reorganization or disarming and disbanding. However, Wang Jizong's part occupies Yajiangqiao and resists orders. This part has more than 2,000 men, including 400-500 men from Liu Guitang's bandit part, with complete firearms, making the future reorganization difficult. (23rd Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yutian letter: It was previously reported that after Wang Qingfang, Zhang Han and other bandit parts in the Lincang area of Yutian withdrew from the town, they fled to the Sanhe County along the Pingyu Road. Zhou Yuying's security team stationed in Yutian has sent a team to suppress them. The two parts now only have about a hundred men. Kuwata, a secretary from the Tangshan Japanese consular branch, has gone to Yutian to investigate and is scheduled to come to the county from Tangshan on the 24th. (23rd Dispatch)

Liu Xiang Telegraphed Victory to the Capital

(Nanjing) Chongqing, 23rd dispatch: Liu Xiang telegraphed to the capital that after Chairman Chiang arrived in Chongqing, the situation in Sichuan Province had changed greatly. He urged unification, strictly enforced opium prohibition, and rectified the police administration, which were very effective. After the Sichuan army recovered Renhuai Moutai, they fought fiercely with the bandit rearguard of more than a thousand men from Maotai Xiang Chishui River to Caozhiwai. The bandits attacked our Zhenlongshan defense line in large numbers and were soundly defeated by our Xie regiment. The bandits retreated to Jianzhuping, with more than two hundred bandits killed. They are now being pursued in different directions. Recently, Xu Xiangqian's bandits in the north have transferred their main force and launched a counterattack against the front of the Fifth Route Army, but they have been repelled. The Third Route Army is also firmly defending its original line and confronting the bandits. There are no other unusual situations. (23rd Dispatch)

Overseas Chinese Village to Beijing Highway; Workers Are Being Recruited to Build

(Nanjing) Qiaole Village in Cixizhen, Xuancheng, Anhui, is building a direct highway to Beijing. The town is 20 li away from Gaochun County. The 180 li highway from Gaochun to Beijing has already been opened to traffic. The Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission is only adding 20 li from Cixi to Gaochun to connect with the Beijing-Chun Highway, which will then lead directly to Beijing. Workers are currently being recruited to build it and it will be completed within the month. After this, the distance between Beijing and the Overseas Chinese will only be a four-hour journey. (23rd Dispatch)

Sangzhi City Completely Recovered; Over 300 Bandits Killed and Countless Items Seized; Remnants Fleeing West, Currently Being Pursued

(Hankou) Chen Yaohan's division of Xu Yuanquan's part captured Sangzhi City on the 22nd. He's fake model division was completely defeated and fled west, and is being pursued. The Hunan army is also fiercely attacking Yongshun, which may be taken within days. Chen Hancun, the director of the Tenth Army's office in Hankou, returned to Hankou by plane on the 23rd after meeting with Xu Yuanquan in Shashi. According to him, the suppression of bandits in the border area of Hunan, Hubei, and Sichuan is progressing rapidly, and it will not be difficult to eliminate the remaining bandits of He and Xiao. (23rd Dispatch)

(Hankou) The 58th Division Chen Yaohan's part telegraphed Hankou on the 22nd saying that Sangzhi had been captured. The telegram stated briefly that Li Jionglin's part attacked Sangzhi at 4:00 AM on the 22nd. The bandits occupying the city, numbering about 3,000, put up a stubborn resistance, but finally collapsed at 5:00 PM and fled west. Our army completely occupied Sangzhi City at 6:30 PM, killing more than 300 bandits and seizing countless items. They are currently pursuing the bandits west of Sangzhi. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Changsha) Li Jue's division has been fiercely suppressing the He and Xiao bandits in Jigongao for days, killing over a thousand bandits. The bandits retreated to Longzhuaguan and fled to the Xu Yan gang's part of bandits in Ping-Liu, which was defeated by the Hunan-Jiangxi armies in Liu Wan and fled south into Pingxiang. (23rd Dispatch)

(Changsha) According to reports, He Long's bandits have fled to the deep mountains of Jingouping in Yongshun, where they have built strong fortifications. On the 18th, our He Yousong brigade bravely attacked and defeated the bandits, killing over 480 bandits and completely destroying the bandit fortifications. In addition, a part of the Red bandits fled to Lou Tangping Yinjiaxi in Dayong. At dawn on the 20th, our Tao Liu brigade and Wang regiment attacked the bandits from both sides, killing more than a hundred bandits and seizing a large number of pseudo-military supplies. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Mei Lanfang Tries His Voice at the Moscow Music Hall; Reports Praise Hu Die's Talent

(Moscow) On the 22nd, Dr. Mei Lanfang gave his first public performance at the Music Hall here, and the seats were packed. Before the opening, the director of the Society for Cultural Exchange with Foreign Countries, Chile Ner Fski, expressed his greetings to the Mei troupe, saying that Mr. Mei is not only a star on the Chinese stage, but also a star on the world stage. "Dr. Mei Lanfang's coming here is extremely important for the development of cultural relations between the great Chinese and Soviet nations," he said. Professor Zhang Pengchun then gave a reply, saying, "We have received a warm and friendly welcome here, and we hope that this kind of understanding will create a foundation for the cultural friendship of our two great countries." On that day, party and government representatives, civil servants, literary and art circles, artists, representatives from various groups in Moscow, and members of the press went to see the show. Mr. Mei then performed "Fenhe Bay," "Fei Zhen'e Assassinating the Tiger," and "Red Thread Stealing the Basin," and the audience welcomed him warmly. (23rd TASS Dispatch)

(Moscow) The Soviet government newspaper Izvestia published an article on the Chinese film star Ms. Hu Die's arrival in the Soviet Union and praised her artistry, calling her one of the few stars with amazing artistic talent. The newspaper also stated, "Ms. Hu's arrival here is to study Soviet films and the work of famous Soviet directors and actors. After staying here for two weeks, she will go to Leningrad to study." (22nd TASS Dispatch)

Song Ziwen will have a Technical Team Accompanying Him when He Goes to Sichuan

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen plans to go to Sichuan around April 10th to inspect economic and transportation construction. In addition to Mr. Song, there will be a technical team accompanying him. The organization of the team is to gather experts in water conservancy, highways, engineering, sericulture, and mining. The selection of personnel is not limited to the Economic Commission, and Mr. Song is selecting from all parties. Before Mr. Song goes to Sichuan, the Economic Commission will first hold an executive meeting to discuss the allocation of funds, as well as to prepare for the team's inspection procedures and areas in Sichuan. (23rd Dispatch)

President Wang Scheduled to Host a Banquet for the British Ambassador

(Nanjing) The British Ambassador, Sir Jada Gan, recently came to Nanjing from Beiping to pay his respects to various authorities of our government and discuss everything. It is now heard that President Wang is scheduled to host a banquet for the Ambassador at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 8:00 PM on the 26th, and the Ambassador is scheduled to host a banquet for Wang and various officials of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at the Embassy at 8:00 PM on the 29th. (23rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ministry of Transportation Settles Overdue Telegram Fees

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Transportation presented to the Executive Yuan that the amount of overdue telegram fees from central party, government, and military agencies is very large. It will calculate the total amount of these overdue payments, transfer it to the Ministry of Finance, and use it as a payment from the Ministry to the national treasury. Relief Measures for Cheap Yarn and Expensive Cotton

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry investigated yarn and cotton prices last year. (Nanjing) The municipal government is implementing measures for household dog registration. Those without a license will be killed. Charitable organizations that keep household dogs must also sterilize them. (23rd Special Dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

Will the United States Really Abandon the Philippines?

— Li

The Philippine Constitution, which began drafting at the end of July last year and was completed in February this year, will be approved by US President Roosevelt today. On the surface, it is a success for the Philippine national independence movement, but in reality, it is a clever application of the United States' hegemonic strategy.

The United States occupied the Philippines after Japan's great victory in the Sino-Japanese War. At that time, the powers were delineating spheres of influence in China, and the United States was unwilling to lag behind. Taking advantage of Spain's weakness and exhaustion, it seized the territory as a base for operating in the Far East. However, the territory is close to Taiwan, which is sufficient to obstruct Japan's ambition to advance south. Therefore, the Japanese resented it deeply. The situation of Japanese-American competition in the Pacific was thus created. Later, Japan formed an alliance with Britain and defeated Tsarist Russia in a major war. Its power gradually increased, while the United States was rich in wealth, and its trade in the Far East also made significant progress. The two sides became evenly matched and competed with each other. When the European War broke out, Japan suddenly occupied the Caroline Islands to cut off the connection between Honolulu and the Philippines. The United States felt greatly threatened and sought ways to deal with it. Intervention at the Paris Peace Conference failed, so it advocated the League of Nations to make the Caroline Islands a mandated territory in an attempt to salvage the situation. Later, the Washington Conference brought together various countries to restrain Japan with international treaties. These are all past events of the United States occupying the Philippines to compete with Japan for hegemony in the Far East.

Today, the situation in the Pacific is quite dangerous, and the United States has expressed its intention to abandon the Philippines. Why is this? It can be said that the United States has never intended to abandon it, but rather to retreat in order to advance. In other words, the United States' governance of colonies is based on the history of its own establishment and its long-standing declarations on international politics, and it always pretends to be enlightened. Japan took advantage of this to promote the Philippine independence movement. This is the first source of the United States' distress and frustration. The United States' mainland and the Philippines are separated by a vast ocean, and it is inherently difficult to defend against the prying eyes of other countries geographically. Japan has already occupied the Caroline Islands and is relentless in its southward advance policy, further threatening the Philippines. This is the second source of the United States' distress and frustration. Since the world economic recession, the United States has gradually become uneasy about the import of Philippine agricultural products and the entry of Filipinos. In the promotion of the recovery movement, it is one of the major problems that urgently needs to be resolved. This is the third source of the United States' distress and frustration. With these three points, coupled with Japan's urgent pursuit of its Asia Monroe Doctrine since the September 18th Incident, the re-establishment of military facilities in the Caroline Islands, and even disregarding everything by withdrawing from the League of Nations and declaring the abandonment of the treaties established at the Washington Conference, the United States was forced by the situation to have this plan to retreat in order to advance.

This is from the perspective of international relations. If we observe it from the perspective of military action, the United States Navy's actions in the Pacific have always been centered on the Panama Canal and San Francisco-Honolulu, focusing on the South Pacific. This year's exercises are being conducted between San Francisco-Honolulu and Alaska, and there is even a proposal to build a port at Dutch Harbor in the Aleutian Islands. The United States' military actions have shifted their focus, and it is natural to make a retreat in the Philippines. However, this is only a retreat and cannot be called abandonment. Although the Taft-McDuffie Act on Philippine independence, which was decided last year, has complied with the Philippine people's request to withdraw the stationed army after the declaration of independence, it still declares that naval bases will be temporarily retained. Moreover, since the Taft-McDuffie Act began to be implemented, the United States has never relaxed its control over the Philippines politically. The national defense plan proposed by the Philippine Constitutional Convention was returned by Governor Murphy, stating that the United States is still responsible for protection until the Philippines is fully independent and that national defense issues are not yet essential. What is the meaning of this move? It is clear to anyone with intelligence. Moreover, the constitution clearly stipulates that after the establishment of a republican government in the Philippines, it will still recognize the sovereignty of the United States, and officials must swear allegiance to the United States. What independence is this? It is better to say that in the economic field, its control methods are even more advanced. The policy of controlling imported goods and adopting a proportional system will be implemented by the republican government to protect American goods and exclude Japanese goods. As for the restrictions on Filipinos going to the United States, the forced management of Philippine cotton production, the prohibition of Philippine sugar imports into the United States, and the recent temporary suspension of business talks between the Philippine delegation to the United States and American officials, it is even more evident that the United States is using the fine name of granting independence to the Philippines to resolve the above-mentioned triple distress with one stroke.

Therefore, we believe that the US President's approval of the Philippine Constitution is a considerable success for the Philippine national movement, and we deeply sympathize with its spirit of fighting for national independence and freedom. However, at the same time, we cannot but point out that the United States has no intention of completely abandoning the Philippines, and the United States' granting of independence to the Philippines is not enough to resolve the disputes and problems between Japan and the United States in the Pacific.

Tokyo Officially Signed the Illegal Agreement on the Chinese Eastern Railway Yesterday, with an Initial Payment of 23.3 Million Yuan, and the Puppet State Will Entrust the South Manchuria Railway Company to Take Over

(Tokyo) The formal signing ceremony of the Chinese Eastern Railway transfer agreement was held at the Foreign Minister's official residence today. On the Japanese side, Foreign Minister Hirota, Vice-Minister Shigemitsu, Director of the European and Asian Affairs Bureau Togo, and Director of the Commercial Bureau Kurusu attended. On the "Manchukuo" side, Minister Ding and Vice-Minister Ohashi attended. On the Soviet side, Ambassador Yurenev, Kazinovsky, and Kizlerzov attended. It was completed at 11:00 a.m. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) The underwriting bank group of the "Manchukuo" national debt issued a check for 23.3 million yuan at 9:30 a.m. on the 23rd. This check was handed over to the Soviet representative by the "Manchukuo" representative as the first payment. The Soviet representative sent it to the Yokohama Specie Bank to convert it into pounds sterling and remit it to the London branch. The payment procedure was thus completed. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Harbin) The last board meeting of the Chinese Eastern Railway was held yesterday afternoon. Chairman Li Shaogeng and six other members attended. Ding Jianxiu, Minister of Communications of "Manchukuo," also attended. It was decided to dissolve the board of directors and the secretariat, and at the same time abolish the post of Director-General. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

(Boli) The entire eastern line of the Chinese Eastern Railway was completely taken over at 10:00 a.m. today and renamed the Bin-Sui Line. At the time of the takeover, a high alert had been in place since the 19th. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

(Manzhouli) The armored train used for the takeover of the western line of the Chinese Eastern Railway successively took over various stations and affiliated buildings. It arrived safely in Manzhouli at 10:00 a.m. After the takeover was completed, the old and new station staff shook hands with each other, and the Soviet red flag was lowered from the station head and replaced with the "Manchukuo" flag. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

(Harbin) The entire 1,700-kilometer approach work of the Chinese Eastern Railway was completed safely near noon on March 23. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

The Process of the Formal Signing

(Tokyo) The agreement on the sale and purchase of the Chinese Eastern Railway and other related documents were formally signed at the Foreign Minister's official residence in Tokyo at 9:30 a.m. on the 23rd. On the Japanese side, Plenipotentiary Minister Hirota and Vice-Minister Shigemitsu, as well as the head of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, attended. On the Soviet side, Plenipotentiary Minister Yurenev, Minister of the Far East Kozlovsky, and attendants attended. On the "Manchukuo" side, Plenipotentiary Minister Ding Shiyuan and Vice-Minister Ohashi, as well as more than 40 other people, attended. The signing was carried out in the following order:

(1) Exchange of credentials of plenipotentiary commissioners of Japan, Manchukuo, and Russia, and inspection of their contents.

(2) The Russian and Manchu plenipotentiaries sign the basic agreement on the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway.

(3) The Russian and Manchu plenipotentiaries sign the protocol between Russia and Manchu.

(4) The "Manchukuo" plenipotentiary hands over to the Soviet Russian plenipotentiary a cash payment of 23 million yuan out of the 140 million yuan purchase price and Manchukuo bonds.

(5) The plenipotentiaries of Japan, Russia, and Manchukuo sign the tripartite protocol on the determination of prices.

(6) The Japanese and Manchu plenipotentiaries sign the exchange of documents between Japan and Manchu regarding the Japanese government's guarantee of payment.

(7) The Japanese and Russian plenipotentiaries sign the exchange of documents between Japan and Russia regarding the Japanese government's guarantee of payment. By 10:15 a.m., the signing of all documents was completely completed. Foreign Minister Hirota then stood up to deliver a congratulatory speech, which was translated into Russian by Director Miyakawa and into "Manchu" by translator Harada. After the Foreign Minister finished his speech, Russian Minister Yurenev and Manchu Minister Ding Shiyuan stood up to express their gratitude. All the plenipotentiaries and attendants raised their glasses together and shouted "Long live!" The entire ceremony was completed at 11:00 a.m. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

Hirota's Address

Foreign Minister Hirota delivered the following speech at the signing ceremony of the Chinese Eastern Railway agreement today: The negotiation on the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway issue has lasted for 21 months and has finally been fully completed. The signing of the relevant documents today will definitely make a great contribution to the promotion of peace in East Asia and the world. I am extremely pleased. The relationship between Russia and Manchukuo will enter a new era with the establishment of this agreement. I hope that friendly relations will increase, and the world in East Asia will become brighter as a result. This is truly the result of the Soviet Russian government's firm determination to resolve the Chinese Eastern Railway issue and the spirit of cooperation of the "Manchukuo" government. The Japanese government has been in the middle, and has been enthusiastically mediating to make the negotiation possible. This is what I, the Minister, am most pleased about. When we think of the important significance of this negotiation, the various twists and turns and difficulties of the past two years are not worth mentioning. In addition to the Chinese Eastern Railway issue, there are still various pending issues between Japan, Russia, and Manchukuo. However, I firmly believe that if we conduct negotiations with the spirit of harmony and cooperation demonstrated in this negotiation, then a satisfactory solution will not be difficult. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

Russian Minister's Thanks

(Tokyo) Soviet Ambassador Yurenev issued a statement today, saying that the completion of the signing of the Eastern Railway agreement between the Soviet and Manchu representatives today is a cause for joy for all peace-loving people in the world. The Soviet government attaches special significance to the improvement of Japanese-Soviet relations. Foreign Minister Hirota's active mediation of this negotiation was a key factor in the success of this negotiation. I am deeply grateful. I am convinced that good faith and mutual trust will guarantee the strengthening of Japanese-Soviet relations in the future. (23rd Dentsu Telegram)

South Manchuria Railway Entrusted to Operate

After the official signing ceremony was completed on the 23rd, the South Manchuria Railway Company will receive an order from the "Manchukuo" government to operate the Chinese Eastern Railway. The South Manchuria Railway authorities issued the following statement: As a result of the agreement reached between Russia and Manchukuo, the Chinese Eastern Railway is now wholly owned by "Manchukuo." The "Manchukuo" government believes that it is most appropriate for the South Manchuria Railway, which is familiar with the railway business, to operate the state-owned railway. It has previously entrusted this company to operate all domestic railways. Now, it has entrusted the South Manchuria Railway to operate the Chinese Eastern Railway. This will not only unify all the railways in Manchuria under a single company, but also maximize economic and technical efficiency. It will definitely make a significant contribution to the development of transportation and industry. This is the reason why the "Manchukuo" government entrusted the South Manchuria Railway to operate the Chinese Eastern Railway, and the South Manchuria Railway has no reason to refuse. Therefore, it has decided to accept the entrustment. (The content of the contract signed between the "Manchukuo" government and the South Manchuria Railway authorities is omitted.) (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Tokyo) The Chinese Eastern Railway's previous freight rates were based on Vladivostok and had many types and complicated calculations. Not only were the railway staff burdened with tedious tasks, but also the business of merchants was greatly inconvenienced. The South Manchuria Railway authorities believe that this price list is not in line with the "Manchukuo"'s principle of equal opportunity for opening up. They decided to sacrifice millions of yuan in profit each year and reduce freight rates. A new price list was released on the 23rd and applied immediately. The result is that the first-class ticket from Changchun to Harbin is reduced by 5.7 yuan, the second-class ticket is reduced by 1.6 yuan, and the third-class ticket is reduced by 1.02 yuan. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Harbin) Harbin Railway Bureau Director Sawara Kenji issued a proclamation on the 23rd, stating that the Chinese Eastern Railway is entrusted by the "Manchukuo" government to the Railway General Bureau to manage all affairs, and is under the management of the Harbin Railway Bureau and will continue to operate. Manchu railway employees will be railway bureau employees from this day on and will have their status guaranteed. However, Russian railway employees will resign from their positions within three months in accordance with the agreement. However, those who resign will be fully paid their retirement benefits, deposits, and allowances. Those who wish to retain their original positions may continue to be employed. Connecting adjacent railways and developing local culture and industry are the important missions of this railway. It is hoped that all employees will be responsible and fulfill their duties. Violators will be punished in accordance with national law. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

Handover

(Harbin) The Chinese Eastern Railway has now been renamed the North Manchuria Railway. The original Russian-Manchu board of directors held its final meeting this morning. The meeting received a telegram from Changchun stating that after the transfer agreement was officially signed in Tokyo, the "Manchu" Minister of Communications Ding Jianxi declared the dissolution of the board of directors, and Li Shaogeng and the Russian side, Bandura, each read the confirmation bulletin of their respective governments. The Russian-Manchu flag hanging in the building was then lowered and replaced with the "Manchu" flag. At the same time, the handover was completed. The new appointees have taken over all stations on the southern, eastern, and western sections. (23rd Reuters Telegram)

Full Text of the Agreement

(Tokyo) The full text of the Chinese Eastern Railway transfer agreement signed by the plenipotentiary representatives of Japan, Manchukuo, and Russia this morning was released simultaneously in Tokyo, Changchun, and Chisk at 11:00 a.m. This agreement consists of the following six documents:

(1) Basic Agreement on the Transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway between Russia and Manchukuo.

(2) Exchange of Documents between Japan and Russia (Part 1).

(3) Exchange of Documents between Japan and Russia (Part 2).

(4) Protocol.

(5) Final Agreement.

The core of this agreement is the Basic Agreement, the full text of which is as follows:

Agreement between the Union of Soviet Socialist Republics of Russia and "Manchukuo" regarding the Transfer of Rights to the Chinese Eastern Railway to "Manchukuo"

"Manchukuo" and the Soviet Republic of Russia, hoping to resolve the Chinese Eastern Railway issue and contribute to the preservation of peace in the Far East, have appointed the following plenipotentiary commissioners to conclude an agreement to transfer Russia's rights over the Chinese Eastern Railway to "Manchukuo."

List of Russian-Manchu Plenipotentiary Commissioners

Ding Shiyuan, "Manchukuo" Ambassador to Japan,

Ohashi Tadaichi, Vice-Minister of Foreign Affairs,

Wu Zesheng, Counselor of the Director-General's Office of the Chinese Eastern Railway,

Yurenev, Soviet Russian Ambassador to Japan,

Kozlovsky, Minister of the Far East,

Kiznitsov, Chairman of the Chinese Eastern Railway Board of Directors,

The above-mentioned plenipotentiary commissioners presented their credentials, recognized them as valid and proper, and agreed on the following articles:

Article 1 The Soviet Russian government shall transfer all its rights over the Chinese Eastern Railway to "Manchukuo." The "Manchukuo" government shall pay the Russian government 140 million Japanese yen.

Article 2 All Soviet Russian rights over the Chinese Eastern Railway shall be transferred to the "Manchukuo" government immediately after the implementation of this agreement. At the same time, the Chinese Eastern Railway shall be under the complete possession and sole management of the "Manchukuo" government.

Article 3 After the establishment of this agreement, senior Russian officials shall be dismissed immediately, and the records, books, documents, and papers under their control shall be handed over to the new successor agency. (Omitted below)

Article 4 The "Manchukuo" government shall succeed the assets and liabilities of the Chinese Eastern Railway, which were entrusted by the Soviet Russian government to the Japanese Foreign Minister on March 22, 1934, to the "Manchukuo" delegation. (Omitted below)

Article 5 The Soviet Russian government shall permanently have the right to all properties such as the Soviet Russian Consulate General in Harbin, staff residences, elementary schools, and libraries. (Omitted below)

Article 6 "Manchukuo" shall abandon the assets of the Chinese Eastern Railway in Soviet Russian territory, as well as the property of the Beijia Railway in Manzhouli and the property used for the connection of the Ussuri Railway, all of which shall be owned by Soviet Russia.

Article 7 Out of the 140 million Japanese yen mentioned in Article 1 of this agreement, 46.7 million yen shall be paid in cash in accordance with the provisions of Article 8 of this agreement, and the remaining 93.3 million yen shall be paid in goods in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of this agreement.

Article 8 Out of the cash payment of 46.7 million yen stipulated in Article 7 of this agreement, 23.3 million yen shall be delivered after the signing of this agreement, and the remaining 23.4 million yen and interest at 3% per annum shall be paid with "Manchukuo" treasury bonds.

In the event that the price of the Japanese yen against the Swiss franc fluctuates by more than 0.8%, the exchange rate of the Japanese yen shall be changed according to the market price. Article 9 The method of paying for goods stipulated in Article 7 shall be as follows: after the signing of the agreement, the Soviet Russian government shall use products or manufactured goods from Japan and Manchukuo to offset the purchase price. The purchase of goods equivalent to 15.5 million yuan in each of the six installments shall be completed within a period of three years after the signing.

Article 10 When dismissing Russian railway employees, they must be notified three months in advance. After resignation, they should be given two months of additional time. Retired railway employees' families have the right to free transportation of luggage on the Chinese Eastern Railway. (Omitted below)

Article 11 This article details in nine items the methods for returning retirement benefits, allowances, deposits, etc. to railway employees.

Article 12 The Chinese Eastern Railway includes all rights, businesses, and properties belonging to this railway.

Article 13 In order to promote transportation relations between the two countries, the "Manchukuo" government and the Soviet Russian government shall, within three months after the establishment of this agreement, separately agree to stipulate the connection with the Ussuri and Siberian lines, and the Chinese Eastern Railway shall connect with the Soviet Russian Siberian and Ussuri stations at Manzhouli and Suifenhe stations.

Article 14 This agreement shall take effect immediately after signing. Each plenipotentiary commissioner shall sign and seal as evidence. Signed in Tokyo on March 23, 1935. (23rd Reuters Telegram)

Document Guaranteeing Payment

(Tokyo) The content of the exchange of documents between the plenipotentiaries of Japan and Russia regarding the Japanese government's guarantee of payment is as follows: In the event that the "Manchukuo" government encounters difficulties regarding payment matters, the Japanese government shall make all necessary efforts to ensure that the Soviet Union government receives all payments due from the "Manchukuo" government without any loss to the Soviet Union government. (23rd Domei News Agency Telegram)

British Garrison in Hong Kong Conducts Exercise; Army, Navy, and Air Force Participate Fully; Blue and Red Forces Take on Offensive and Defensive Roles Respectively

Britain, France, and Italy Hold Meeting in Paris; Thorough Discussion of the European Situation; Talks Progressing Well; Simon and Eden Fly to Berlin Today; Second Meeting to be Held at Lake Como

(Paris) British Lord Privy Seal Anthony Eden, French Foreign Minister Laval, and Undersecretary Suvich gathered unexpectedly at the French Foreign Ministry at 11:20 this morning. Also in attendance were French Premier Flandin, French Minister of Finance Germain-Martin, and Minister without Portfolio Herriot. It is reported that they thoroughly discussed the overall European situation and Germany's decision to rearm. Before the start of the trilateral discussion, Eden and the British Ambassador to Paris, Clerk, exchanged words with Laval. Shortly after, Suvich arrived with a smile and briefly spoke with Laval as well. The meeting adjourned at noon, and Suvich and Eden dined with Laval. When asked about the meeting's progress, Suvich smiled and did not answer, only saying, "Everything is progressing very well." It is reported that Eden informed the French and Italian diplomatic authorities that the British government proposes to hold a second trilateral meeting at Lake Como after his return to London on April 4th or 5th. If so, the meeting will be delayed until around April 7th. The atmosphere at this morning's meeting was quite optimistic, but no announcements were made after the adjournment. It is rumored that Eden suggested holding a four-power conference in London, "and inviting Germany to participate." This claim was denied by authorities this afternoon. Several experienced observers in London believe that Britain, France, and Italy seem to be engaging in diplomatic discussions with Germany, rather than holding a conference. (Reuters, 23rd)

British Cabinet Minister to Tour Eastern Europe Today

(London) "Lord Privy Seal Anthony Eden, known as Britain's arms reduction advocate," departed for Paris today aboard a specially prepared aircraft. This trip will involve discussing the overall situation in the capitals of four European countries. Key figures such as Soviet Ambassador Maisky were present to see him off. Eden will first meet with French Foreign Minister Laval and Undersecretary Suvich tomorrow, followed by a trip to Berlin. British Foreign Secretary Simon is scheduled to fly to the German capital on Sunday to join in talks with German authorities regarding the situation caused by Germany's rearmament. Simon will then return to London, while Eden will travel to Moscow to meet with Russian authorities, followed by trips to Prague, Warsaw, and Prague in Czechia, before returning to London by air on April 4th. (Reuters, 22nd)

Diplomatic Efforts to Avert Crisis

(London) The British government still believes that the European crisis can be averted through careful and diplomatic means. Lord Privy Seal Anthony Eden departed from London by plane to Paris today to participate in the preliminary meeting of Britain, France, and Italy. Foreign Secretary Simon, accompanied by five staff members, will fly to Berlin tomorrow. At that time, Eden will also join in assisting with meetings with German leader Hitler and Göring. A dispatch from Paris states that French Foreign Minister Laval also believes that war can be avoided through the mediation of diplomats from various countries. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Second Meeting to be Held in Northern Italy

(Geneva) According to today's news, representatives from Britain, France, and Italy will meet in the near future at Lake Como to discuss Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles by rearming. The Italian representative is Premier Mussolini, the French representative is Foreign Minister Laval, and the British representative is Foreign Secretary Simon. Undersecretary Suvich is currently in Paris and will also participate in the meeting. People here are paying close attention to this meeting, as those in attendance will be able to ascertain Germany's true intentions and "address concrete realities." (Reuters, 23rd)

Italian Premier Prepares to Welcome Guests

(Rome) Premier Mussolini is currently preparing to welcome officials from the British and French governments in the coming days. It is reported that Mussolini believes that the signatories of the Treaty of Versailles should take firm steps regarding the treaty's military clauses. Mussolini is very displeased with the German Foreign Ministry's rejection of Italy's protest. Mussolini has not indicated whether he will accept the British invitation for Germany to participate in the upcoming three-power conference in Como, but it is reported that Mussolini will decide on this matter after the conclusion of today's meeting in Paris. (National Telegram, 23rd)

League of Nations to Hold Special Meeting in Early April

(Geneva) The Administrative Council of the League of Nations will meet in the first week of next month in response to France's request to discuss the issue of Germany's rearmament. However, the exact date of the meeting has not yet been determined. (Havas, 22nd)

According to a Reuters dispatch from London, the Administrative Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to meet in the first week of April to discuss France's complaint against Germany's rearmament. Some quarters now feel that the Administrative Council meeting should be held after the Como conference. (Reuters, 23rd)

Hitler Intends to Expand Navy

(Berlin) Officials stated today that during tomorrow's meeting between leader Hitler and British Foreign Secretary Simon, Germany may demand a larger navy in addition to conscription, as Hitler considers the security of the army and navy to be a fundamental policy. If other countries do not recognize this policy, Germany will not return to the League of Nations. If Germany cannot stand on an absolutely equal footing with related countries, it is doubtful that Hitler will accept the air force pact proposed by Britain and France. However, German Foreign Minister Neurath told an Associated Press reporter that the meeting between Foreign Secretary Simon and leader Hitler would benefit all of Europe. The government is eagerly and with great satisfaction awaiting the arrival of the British dignitaries. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Germans Enthusiastically Donate to Military Expenses

(Berlin) Many Germans are donating cash to cover army expenses. Defense Minister General von Blomberg recently opened a special account at a bank in Berlin, named "The People's Expression of Gratitude to the Army." All such donations will be deposited into this account, with all procedures kept extremely simple. (Havas, 22nd)

German Navy Improves Torpedoes; Propelled by Electricity, Leaves No Wake

(London) The Daily Telegraph reports that the German Navy has made significant improvements to its torpedoes. In the future, they will be propelled by electricity, leaving no trace on the surface of the water. Those launched from submarines will use equipment to reduce air, preventing the generation of waves. Research into these electric torpedoes began as early as 1918, and their speed is slightly slower than that of ordinary torpedoes. (Havas, 23rd)

Bound by the Treaty of Versailles; Germany Can No Longer Endure; Entrusts Security to its Own Strength

Port of Hanover, Germany: Propaganda Minister Goebbels delivered a speech here today, stating, "Germany can no longer endure the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles. If we wish to liberate ourselves, we must adopt revolutionary measures in domestic affairs, and their impact will inevitably extend to foreign affairs. This is why the government, on March 16th, entrusted the responsibility of maintaining national security to the strength of the German people themselves." Goebbels then discussed the issue of foreign currency shortages, stating that Germany must import large quantities of raw materials to manufacture industrial products in order to prevent unemployment. This is the reason for imports exceeding exports and the shortage of foreign currency, which the people must endure. (Havas, 23rd)

Italian Premier Encourages Blackshirt Comrades; Maintain Peace with Arms; Orders Conscription; Prepared for Any Eventuality

(Rome) Italian Premier Mussolini delivered a highly impassioned speech to several thousand Blackshirt comrades this afternoon, stating that our desire for peace is rooted in millions of bayonets. We want to be prepared for any situation that may arise in the future and to overcome any obstacles that may prevent us from achieving our goals. (Reuters, 23rd)

(Paris) Representatives from Britain, Italy, and France met at the Foreign Ministry at 11:15 this morning to seek peaceful solutions amid the turmoil caused by Germany's restoration of military clauses. However, according to a report from Rome, Premier Mussolini has ordered the full mobilization of the 1911 class of the army. The mobilization order states that this mobilization is "precautionary" in nature. It is understood that after this military buildup, Italy's standing army has increased to 600,000 men. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Rome) Italy is clearly wary of Germany's rearmament. Today, Italian Premier Mussolini issued an order summoning a large number of conscripts into the army. Approximately half of the 1911 class of conscripts were already called up last month to serve in Italian Somaliland. The remaining individuals were all ordered to be called up today. It is reported that this move will bring the number of Italians bearing arms to 650,000, in addition to the 400,000 members of the Fascist militia armed with rifles and machine guns, bringing the total strength of Italy's armed forces to over one million. (Reuters, 22nd)

Renovating the Navy and Actively Building Ships

(Rome) After deliberating on extending the term of military service yesterday, bringing its army to over 500,000 men, the Italian government announced today that it would expand and renovate its navy. Undersecretary of the Navy Cavagnari recently presented a portion of the navy's shipbuilding plan for the coming year to the National Assembly, stating that in the current fiscal year, Italy plans to improve a number of existing warships, and construct four destroyers, two torpedo boats, and one submarine destroyer. The current three-year naval service may be extended in accordance with army procedures, in order to increase the number of naval personnel and combat power. (National Telegram, 23rd)

French Government Decides to Increase Professional Army; Extends Term of Service for New Recruits

(Paris) The government has decided to temporarily extend the term of service for new recruits within the "deficit years" from October of this year to 1939 to two years. In addition, the government requests that from 1936 to 1940, the age for new recruits to join the army be gradually lowered from 21 to 20. At the same time, it will intensify the recruitment of a professional army. All personnel reorganizations will be carried out within the scope of the 1928 conscription law. This proposal has been submitted to the Chamber of Deputies for review. The Army Committee discussed it yesterday, with Army Minister Maurin personally attending to provide explanations. (Havas, 22nd)

Simon Speaks; Britain is Pragmatic; Devoted to the Cause of Peace; Unwilling to Make Adventurous Attempts

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon stated in a speech near Lichfield, "British people must work together with one heart and one mind on the issue of peace-building. If there are differences of opinion, conflicting goals, and scattered energy, then regardless of the reason, it will not benefit peace. We cannot attempt various adventurous actions in foreign countries, nor can we be bound by anyone's disputes. It must be known that this is not conducive to the cause of peace, and it is contrary to the pragmatic mindset of the British people." (Havas, 22nd)

Germany Assures France and Italy that it Will Not Station Troops in the Rhineland

(Berlin) According to reliable sources, Foreign Minister Neurath, while rejecting the points raised in France's protest letter, offered assurances to the French ambassador that there was no intention to abolish the demilitarized zone in the Rhineland. Subsequently, the same assurances were given to the Italian ambassador. If so, Germany will not station troops in the Rhineland province and within 50 kilometers of the right bank of the Rhine River. Leaders of the National Socialist Party believe that the protest letters from Italy and France are mere empty words, stating that the progress of events cannot be stopped by anything. German sources previously stated that since the right to military equality had been realized, they would no longer oppose returning to Geneva. French political figures deeply believe that this is a new strategy by Germany, hoping that Britain will feel satisfied with this "magnanimous act." (Havas, 22nd)

Little Entente is Highly Wary of Germany; Forms a Solid Common Front; Romanian Foreign Minister to Consult with Britain and France

Bucharest: The Balkan countries currently hold a serious view of Germany's reinstatement of compulsory military service. Diplomatic sources here claim that the Little Entente and the Balkan countries have decided that if former enemy countries follow Germany's lead, they will mobilize. It is reported that a declaration will be issued soon, explaining this decision. (Reuters, 23rd)

Bucharest: Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu held a lengthy conversation with British Minister Hoare today. Hoare explained Britain's views on various important issues in Europe. Titulescu has decided to depart soon for the capital of Yugoslavia and Paris to consult with authorities in both countries, and will also make a trip to Britain. (Havas, 23rd)

Hull Advocates Respect for Treaties; No Less Than a Subtle Criticism of Germany; Generally Believed to be a Prelude to Action

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull stated definitively during a meeting with reporters today the necessity of strictly adhering to various treaties, and said that U.S. officials are closely watching the European situation. Judging from his remarks, they contain the intention of the U.S. government not supporting Germany's rearmament. However, Hull was unwilling to disclose what actions the United States would take. According to observers, Hull's remarks on the dignity of treaties are a prelude to some kind of action by the United States. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Berlin) The Berlin Daily News criticized U.S. Secretary of State Hull's declaration yesterday, stating that the United States should use its spiritual strength to ensure that various treaties are strictly adhered to. The newspaper said Hull's words are "voicing support for French extremism" and are a subtle criticism of Germany. It is understood that "although Germany recognizes that treaties can establish peace in Europe, there are many different kinds of treaties and they cannot be generalized." (Havas, 22nd)

Conflicting Opinions Among Americans

(Washington) Senator Pittman, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, stated that the United States is not a member of the League of Nations, so the issue of Germany's rearmament should be completely ignored. However, another member of the committee, Democrat Pope, stated that under the current circumstances, if war breaks out in Europe, the United States would be unable to maintain neutrality, and domestic industrialists and cotton planters would inevitably exert strong pressure on the government and Congress to ensure that maritime trade routes remain unobstructed (meaning maintaining the principle of freedom of the seas). (Havas, 22nd)

Following Germany's Lead; Austria Rearms; Existing Standing Army is Insufficient to Cope with Events; France Will Assist in Forming a Military Plan to Encircle Germany

(Vienna) Austria joined the rearmament movement today. The Department of the Army has summoned all reserve officers for training in order to train a powerful new army. These officers have been ordered to report by March 30th. Specific plans have not been announced, but unofficial sources claim that the government is planning to restore nationwide conscription soon. However, observers express skepticism about Austria following Germany's lead in rearming. It is understood that the government believes that other major powers have increased their military strength, and therefore it cannot deny Austria the right to expand its military organization. Austria currently has a standing army of 30,000 men. Premier Schuschnigg believes that this is insufficient to cope with any major events. Current government officials are indeed friendly with France and Britain and oppose Hitler's policies. They have great influence over Austria's rearmament plan. It is said that France will help Austria obtain a larger army in order to complete its military plan to encircle Germany. (National Telegram, 23rd)

(Vienna) The Council of State met today to discuss the international situation. As a result, it was agreed that Austria's defense capabilities needed to be strengthened, and the government would conduct negotiations with other countries in order to achieve the right to military equality. Today, air defense exercises were held near the cities of Neustadt and Baden, with the participation of the federal army, police, all health organizations, and various military and civilian organizations. (Havas, 22nd)

Soviet Russia Desires Peace; Strong Enough to Resist Foreign Aggression; Declaration by Russian Ambassador to the United States

(New York) Soviet Ambassador to the United States Troyanovsky issued a declaration, stating that if war breaks out in Europe, its consequences will inevitably spread globally. The Soviet Union is now prepared to guarantee its territorial integrity so that it will not be invaded by other countries, but the Soviet Union desires peace and will never invade others. He also stated that the Soviet Union is willing to expand trade with the United States, hoping to strengthen relations between the two countries. (Havas, 22nd)

Russia Expands Merchant Fleet; Purchases Twenty Ships from Dutch Merchants

Amsterdam: According to today's news report from Rotterdam, Soviet Russia has formulated a plan to expand its merchant fleet and is currently negotiating with Dutch shipowners to purchase 20 transport ships, including seven ships owned by the Dutch Lloyd Company. According to the company, a deal has not yet been reached, but well-informed sources say that it has already been completed. (Reuters, 22nd)

U.S. House of Representatives Committee Passes Bill to Build Air Bases

(Washington) Representative Vinson, Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, stated that the government would allocate $38 million from the $300 million public works budget for 1936 to construct air bases at Pearl Harbor in the Hawaiian Islands, the west coast of the United States, and the Panama Canal Zone. It is now understood that this bill will be submitted to the House of Representatives for discussion next Tuesday. The Navy currently has 1,000 aircraft and is now requesting to double that number, but there is a severe shortage of pilots, which needs to be addressed. Furthermore, legislation to construct army air bases along the Atlantic coast, the northeast and southeast corners of the Pacific, northwestern Alaska, and its interior has been passed by a vote of the House Army Committee. (Havas, 22nd)

U.S. Mystery Aircraft; Test Flight to Honolulu Cancelled

(Washington) The United States' machine-piloted aircraft, intended for a test flight to Honolulu, had been prepared for a long time and had been widely publicized, but today the Department of Commerce's Bureau of Air Commerce suddenly announced its cancellation. It is also reported that future test flights are planned to be held in the Atlantic Ocean. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Zeppelin Airline Company Established; Göring Appointed Chairman

(Berlin) The Zeppelin Airline Company was officially established today, with Aviation Minister Göring as the chairman. Dr. Eckener, the former captain of the Zeppelin airships that traveled between Europe and the United States, is the chairman of the supervisory committee. The company will be responsible for transporting passengers, goods, and mail on several routes. (Havas-Kayala, 23rd)

(Berlin) A meeting was held here today, chaired by Aviation Minister General Göring, to decide on the establishment of an airship transport company for passengers and goods, named the German Zeppelin Transport Company. The headquarters is located in Berlin, with a fixed capital of 9.95 million marks. The Friedrichshafen Zeppelin Airship Manufacturing Company has subscribed to 5.7 million marks, and the Hansa Company has subscribed to 3.85 million marks. The well-known commander of the large Zeppelin airship, Dr. Eckener, has been appointed as the general manager. (Reuters, 22nd)

Mexico Orders Gold to be Nationalized

Mexico City: The President issued an order today that all gold holdings must be processed by the Bank of Mexico, and all gold sales must also be handled by the bank. Although the order does not explicitly stipulate the confiscation of people's gold holdings, it is practically equivalent to implementing a national gold policy. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Russian Youth Gang Commits Crimes for "Fun"; Theft Discovered, Leader Executed

(Moscow) A group of young people dedicated themselves to committing crimes and established a general association to train children in the skills of theft. Recently, they were discovered, and their three leaders, all between the ages of eighteen and twenty, were executed. During the interrogation, the individuals confessed that they were not stealing due to poverty, but for "fun." One accomplice, under the age of twenty, was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment. A sixteen-year-old female, who served as a "lookout," was sentenced to five years of imprisonment. Recently, the authorities launched a major campaign to eliminate bandits nationwide. Thousands of workers have volunteered as assistants, and 4,000 bandits and 2,000 petty thieves have been arrested in Leningrad alone. (Reuters, 23rd)
